8 /// ----
9 /// \file ----
10 /// Post-legalization lowering for instructions. ----
11 /// ----
12 /// This is used to offload pattern matching from the selector. ----
13 /// ----
14 /// For example, this combiner will notice that a G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR is actually ----
15 /// a G_ZIP, G_UZP, etc. ----
16 /// ----
17 /// General optimization combines should be handled by either the ----
18 /// AArch64PostLegalizerCombiner or the AArch64PreLegalizerCombiner. ----
19 /// ----
20 //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===// ----

67 /// Represents a pseudo instruction which replaces a G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR. ----
68 /// ----
69 /// Used for matching target-supported shuffles before codegen. ----
70 struct ShuffleVectorPseudo { ----
71 unsigned Opc; ///< Opcode for the instruction. (E.g. G_ZIP1) ----
72 Register Dst; ///< Destination register. ----
73 SmallVector SrcOps; ///< Source registers. ----
74 ShuffleVectorPseudo(unsigned Opc, Register Dst, 0
75 std::initializer_list SrcOps) ----
76 : Opc(Opc), Dst(Dst), SrcOps(SrcOps){}; 0
77 ShuffleVectorPseudo() = default; 0
78 }; ----

80 /// Check if a vector shuffle corresponds to a REV instruction with the ----
81 /// specified blocksize. ----
82 bool isREVMask(ArrayRef M, unsigned EltSize, unsigned NumElts, 0
83 unsigned BlockSize) { ----
84 assert((BlockSize == 16 || BlockSize == 32 || BlockSize == 64) && 0
85 "Only possible block sizes for REV are: 16, 32, 64"); ----
86 assert(EltSize != 64 && "EltSize cannot be 64 for REV mask."); 0
87 ----
88 unsigned BlockElts = M[0] + 1; 0
89 ----
90 // If the first shuffle index is UNDEF, be optimistic. ----
91 if (M[0] < 0) 0
92 BlockElts = BlockSize / EltSize; 0
93 ----
94 if (BlockSize <= EltSize || BlockSize != BlockElts * EltSize) 0
95 return false; 0
96 ----
97 for (unsigned i = 0; i < NumElts; ++i) { 0
98 // Ignore undef indices. ----
99 if (M[i] < 0) 0
100 continue; 0
101 if (static_cast(M[i]) != 0
102 (i - i % BlockElts) + (BlockElts - 1 - i % BlockElts)) 0
103 return false; 0
104 } ----
105 ----
106 return true; 0
107 } ----

109 /// Determines if \p M is a shuffle vector mask for a TRN of \p NumElts. ----
110 /// Whether or not G_TRN1 or G_TRN2 should be used is stored in \p WhichResult. ----
111 bool isTRNMask(ArrayRef M, unsigned NumElts, unsigned &WhichResult) { 0
112 if (NumElts % 2 != 0) 0
113 return false; 0
114 WhichResult = (M[0] == 0 ? 0 : 1); 0
115 for (unsigned i = 0; i < NumElts; i += 2) { 0
116 if ((M[i] >= 0 && static_cast(M[i]) != i + WhichResult) || 0
117 (M[i + 1] >= 0 && 0
118 static_cast(M[i + 1]) != i + NumElts + WhichResult)) 0
119 return false; 0
120 } ----
121 return true; 0
122 } ----

124 /// Check if a G_EXT instruction can handle a shuffle mask \p M when the vector ----
125 /// sources of the shuffle are different. ----
126 std::optional> getExtMask(ArrayRef M, 0
127 unsigned NumElts) { ----
128 // Look for the first non-undef element. ----
129 auto FirstRealElt = find_if(M, [](int Elt) { return Elt >= 0; }); 0
130 if (FirstRealElt == M.end()) 0
131 return std::nullopt; 0
132 ----
133 // Use APInt to handle overflow when calculating expected element. ----
134 unsigned MaskBits = APInt(32, NumElts * 2).logBase2(); 0
135 APInt ExpectedElt = APInt(MaskBits, *FirstRealElt + 1); 0
136 ----
137 // The following shuffle indices must be the successive elements after the ----
138 // first real element. ----
139 if (any_of( 0
140 make_range(std::next(FirstRealElt), M.end()), 0
141 [&ExpectedElt](int Elt) { return Elt != ExpectedElt++ && Elt >= 0; })) 0
142 return std::nullopt; 0
143 ----
144 // The index of an EXT is the first element if it is not UNDEF. ----
145 // Watch out for the beginning UNDEFs. The EXT index should be the expected ----
146 // value of the first element. E.g. ----
147 // <-1, -1, 3, ...> is treated as <1, 2, 3, ...>. ----
148 // <-1, -1, 0, 1, ...> is treated as <2*NumElts-2, 2*NumElts-1, 0, 1, ...>. ----
149 // ExpectedElt is the last mask index plus 1. ----
150 uint64_t Imm = ExpectedElt.getZExtValue(); 0
151 bool ReverseExt = false; 0
152 ----
153 // There are two difference cases requiring to reverse input vectors. ----
154 // For example, for vector <4 x i32> we have the following cases, ----
155 // Case 1: shufflevector(<4 x i32>,<4 x i32>,<-1, -1, -1, 0>) ----
156 // Case 2: shufflevector(<4 x i32>,<4 x i32>,<-1, -1, 7, 0>) ----
157 // For both cases, we finally use mask <5, 6, 7, 0>, which requires ----
158 // to reverse two input vectors. ----
159 if (Imm < NumElts) 0
160 ReverseExt = true; 0
161 else ----
162 Imm -= NumElts; 0
163 return std::make_pair(ReverseExt, Imm); 0
164 } 0
165 ----
166 /// Determines if \p M is a shuffle vector mask for a UZP of \p NumElts. ----
167 /// Whether or not G_UZP1 or G_UZP2 should be used is stored in \p WhichResult. ----
168 bool isUZPMask(ArrayRef M, unsigned NumElts, unsigned &WhichResult) { 0
169 WhichResult = (M[0] == 0 ? 0 : 1); 0
170 for (unsigned i = 0; i != NumElts; ++i) { 0
171 // Skip undef indices. ----
172 if (M[i] < 0) 0
173 continue; 0
174 if (static_cast(M[i]) != 2 * i + WhichResult) 0
175 return false; 0
176 } ----
177 return true; 0
178 } ----
179 ----
180 /// \return true if \p M is a zip mask for a shuffle vector of \p NumElts. ----
181 /// Whether or not G_ZIP1 or G_ZIP2 should be used is stored in \p WhichResult. ----
182 bool isZipMask(ArrayRef M, unsigned NumElts, unsigned &WhichResult) { 0
183 if (NumElts % 2 != 0) 0
184 return false; 0
185 ----
186 // 0 means use ZIP1, 1 means use ZIP2. ----
187 WhichResult = (M[0] == 0 ? 0 : 1); 0
188 unsigned Idx = WhichResult * NumElts / 2; 0
189 for (unsigned i = 0; i != NumElts; i += 2) { 0
190 if ((M[i] >= 0 && static_cast(M[i]) != Idx) || 0
191 (M[i + 1] >= 0 && static_cast(M[i + 1]) != Idx + NumElts)) 0
192 return false; 0
193 Idx += 1; 0
194 } ----
195 return true; 0
196 } ----

198 /// Helper function for matchINS. ----
199 /// ----
200 /// \returns a value when \p M is an ins mask for \p NumInputElements. ----
201 /// ----
202 /// First element of the returned pair is true when the produced ----
203 /// G_INSERT_VECTOR_ELT destination should be the LHS of the G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR. ----
204 /// ----
205 /// Second element is the destination lane for the G_INSERT_VECTOR_ELT. ----
206 std::optional> isINSMask(ArrayRef M, 0
207 int NumInputElements) { ----
208 if (M.size() != static_cast(NumInputElements)) 0
209 return std::nullopt; 0
210 int NumLHSMatch = 0, NumRHSMatch = 0; 0
211 int LastLHSMismatch = -1, LastRHSMismatch = -1; 0
212 for (int Idx = 0; Idx < NumInputElements; ++Idx) { 0
213 if (M[Idx] == -1) { 0
214 ++NumLHSMatch; 0
215 ++NumRHSMatch; 0
216 continue; 0
217 } ----
218 M[Idx] == Idx ? ++NumLHSMatch : LastLHSMismatch = Idx; 0
219 M[Idx] == Idx + NumInputElements ? ++NumRHSMatch : LastRHSMismatch = Idx; 0
220 } ----
221 const int NumNeededToMatch = NumInputElements - 1; 0
222 if (NumLHSMatch == NumNeededToMatch) 0
223 return std::make_pair(true, LastLHSMismatch); 0
224 if (NumRHSMatch == NumNeededToMatch) 0
225 return std::make_pair(false, LastRHSMismatch); 0
226 return std::nullopt; 0
227 } ----

229 /// \return true if a G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR instruction \p MI can be replaced with a ----
230 /// G_REV instruction. Returns the appropriate G_REV opcode in \p Opc. ----
231 bool matchREV(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
232 ShuffleVectorPseudo &MatchInfo) { ----
233 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR); 0
234 ArrayRef ShuffleMask = MI.getOperand(3).getShuffleMask(); 0
235 Register Dst = MI.getOperand(0).getReg(); 0
236 Register Src = MI.getOperand(1).getReg(); 0
237 LLT Ty = MRI.getType(Dst); 0
238 unsigned EltSize = Ty.getScalarSizeInBits(); 0
239 ----
240 // Element size for a rev cannot be 64. ----
241 if (EltSize == 64) 0
242 return false; 0
243 ----
244 unsigned NumElts = Ty.getNumElements(); 0
245 ----
246 // Try to produce G_REV64 ----
247 if (isREVMask(ShuffleMask, EltSize, NumElts, 64)) { 0
248 MatchInfo = ShuffleVectorPseudo(AArch64::G_REV64, Dst, {Src}); 0
249 return true; 0
250 } ----
251 ----
252 // TODO: Produce G_REV32 and G_REV16 once we have proper legalization support. ----
253 // This should be identical to above, but with a constant 32 and constant ----
254 // 16. ----
255 return false; 0
256 } ----

313 /// Helper function for matchDup. ----
314 bool matchDupFromInsertVectorElt(int Lane, MachineInstr &MI, 0
315 MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, ----
316 ShuffleVectorPseudo &MatchInfo) { ----
317 if (Lane != 0) 0
318 return false; 0
319 ----
320 // Try to match a vector splat operation into a dup instruction. ----
321 // We're looking for this pattern: ----
322 // ----
323 // %scalar:gpr(s64) = COPY $x0 ----
324 // %undef:fpr(<2 x s64>) = G_IMPLICIT_DEF ----
325 // %cst0:gpr(s32) = G_CONSTANT i32 0 ----
326 // %zerovec:fpr(<2 x s32>) = G_BUILD_VECTOR %cst0(s32), %cst0(s32) ----
327 // %ins:fpr(<2 x s64>) = G_INSERT_VECTOR_ELT %undef, %scalar(s64), %cst0(s32) ----
328 // %splat:fpr(<2 x s64>) = G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR %ins(<2 x s64>), %undef, ----
329 // %zerovec(<2 x s32>) ----
330 // ----
331 // ...into: ----
332 // %splat = G_DUP %scalar ----
333 ----
334 // Begin matching the insert. ----
335 auto *InsMI = getOpcodeDef(TargetOpcode::G_INSERT_VECTOR_ELT, 0
336 MI.getOperand(1).getReg(), MRI); 0
337 if (!InsMI) 0
338 return false; 0
339 // Match the undef vector operand. ----
340 if (!getOpcodeDef(TargetOpcode::G_IMPLICIT_DEF, InsMI->getOperand(1).getReg(), 0
341 MRI)) ----
342 return false; 0
343 ----
344 // Match the index constant 0. ----
345 if (!mi_match(InsMI->getOperand(3).getReg(), MRI, m_ZeroInt())) 0
346 return false; 0
347 ----
348 MatchInfo = ShuffleVectorPseudo(AArch64::G_DUP, MI.getOperand(0).getReg(), 0
349 {InsMI->getOperand(2).getReg()}); 0
350 return true; 0
351 } ----

353 /// Helper function for matchDup. ----
354 bool matchDupFromBuildVector(int Lane, MachineInstr &MI, 0
355 MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, ----
356 ShuffleVectorPseudo &MatchInfo) { ----
357 assert(Lane >= 0 && "Expected positive lane?"); 0
358 // Test if the LHS is a BUILD_VECTOR. If it is, then we can just reference the ----
359 // lane's definition directly. ----
360 auto *BuildVecMI = getOpcodeDef(TargetOpcode::G_BUILD_VECTOR, 0
361 MI.getOperand(1).getReg(), MRI); 0
362 if (!BuildVecMI) 0
363 return false; 0
364 Register Reg = BuildVecMI->getOperand(Lane + 1).getReg(); 0
365 MatchInfo = ----
366 ShuffleVectorPseudo(AArch64::G_DUP, MI.getOperand(0).getReg(), {Reg}); 0
367 return true; 0
368 } ----
369 ----
370 bool matchDup(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
371 ShuffleVectorPseudo &MatchInfo) { ----
372 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR); 0
373 auto MaybeLane = getSplatIndex(MI); 0
374 if (!MaybeLane) 0
375 return false; 0
376 int Lane = *MaybeLane; 0
377 // If this is undef splat, generate it via "just" vdup, if possible. ----
378 if (Lane < 0) 0
379 Lane = 0; 0
380 if (matchDupFromInsertVectorElt(Lane, MI, MRI, MatchInfo)) 0
381 return true; 0
382 if (matchDupFromBuildVector(Lane, MI, MRI, MatchInfo)) 0
383 return true; 0
384 return false; 0
385 } ----

387 // Check if an EXT instruction can handle the shuffle mask when the vector ----
388 // sources of the shuffle are the same. ----
389 bool isSingletonExtMask(ArrayRef M, LLT Ty) { 0
390 unsigned NumElts = Ty.getNumElements(); 0
391 ----
392 // Assume that the first shuffle index is not UNDEF. Fail if it is. ----
393 if (M[0] < 0) 0
394 return false; 0
395 ----
396 // If this is a VEXT shuffle, the immediate value is the index of the first ----
397 // element. The other shuffle indices must be the successive elements after ----
398 // the first one. ----
399 unsigned ExpectedElt = M[0]; 0
400 for (unsigned I = 1; I < NumElts; ++I) { 0
401 // Increment the expected index. If it wraps around, just follow it ----
402 // back to index zero and keep going. ----
403 ++ExpectedElt; 0
404 if (ExpectedElt == NumElts) 0
405 ExpectedElt = 0; 0
406 ----
407 if (M[I] < 0) 0
408 continue; // Ignore UNDEF indices. 0
409 if (ExpectedElt != static_cast(M[I])) 0
410 return false; 0
411 } ----
412 ----
413 return true; 0
414 } ----

416 bool matchEXT(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
417 ShuffleVectorPseudo &MatchInfo) { ----
418 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR); 0
419 Register Dst = MI.getOperand(0).getReg(); 0
420 LLT DstTy = MRI.getType(Dst); 0
421 Register V1 = MI.getOperand(1).getReg(); 0
422 Register V2 = MI.getOperand(2).getReg(); 0
423 auto Mask = MI.getOperand(3).getShuffleMask(); 0
424 uint64_t Imm; ----
425 auto ExtInfo = getExtMask(Mask, DstTy.getNumElements()); 0
426 uint64_t ExtFactor = MRI.getType(V1).getScalarSizeInBits() / 8; 0
427 ----
428 if (!ExtInfo) { 0
429 if (!getOpcodeDef(V2, MRI) || 0
430 !isSingletonExtMask(Mask, DstTy)) 0
431 return false; 0
432 ----
433 Imm = Mask[0] * ExtFactor; 0
434 MatchInfo = ShuffleVectorPseudo(AArch64::G_EXT, Dst, {V1, V1, Imm}); 0
435 return true; 0
436 } ----
437 bool ReverseExt; ----
438 std::tie(ReverseExt, Imm) = *ExtInfo; 0
439 if (ReverseExt) 0
440 std::swap(V1, V2); 0
441 Imm *= ExtFactor; 0
442 MatchInfo = ShuffleVectorPseudo(AArch64::G_EXT, Dst, {V1, V2, Imm}); 0
443 return true; 0
444 } ----

451 MIRBuilder.buildInstr(MatchInfo.Opc, {MatchInfo.Dst}, MatchInfo.SrcOps); 0
452 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
453 } 0

455 /// Replace a G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR instruction with G_EXT. ----
456 /// Special-cased because the constant operand must be emitted as a G_CONSTANT ----
457 /// for the imported tablegen patterns to work. ----
458 void applyEXT(MachineInstr &MI, ShuffleVectorPseudo &MatchInfo) { 0
459 MachineIRBuilder MIRBuilder(MI); 0
460 // Tablegen patterns expect an i32 G_CONSTANT as the final op. ----
461 auto Cst = ----
462 MIRBuilder.buildConstant(LLT::scalar(32), MatchInfo.SrcOps[2].getImm()); 0
463 MIRBuilder.buildInstr(MatchInfo.Opc, {MatchInfo.Dst}, 0
464 {MatchInfo.SrcOps[0], MatchInfo.SrcOps[1], Cst}); 0
465 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
466 } 0
467 ----
468 /// Match a G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR with a mask which corresponds to a ----
469 /// G_INSERT_VECTOR_ELT and G_EXTRACT_VECTOR_ELT pair. ----
470 /// ----
471 /// e.g. ----
472 /// %shuf = G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR %left, %right, shufflemask(0, 0) ----
473 /// ----
474 /// Can be represented as ----
475 /// ----
476 /// %extract = G_EXTRACT_VECTOR_ELT %left, 0 ----
477 /// %ins = G_INSERT_VECTOR_ELT %left, %extract, 1 ----
478 /// ----
479 bool matchINS(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
480 std::tuple &MatchInfo) { ----
481 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR); 0
482 ArrayRef ShuffleMask = MI.getOperand(3).getShuffleMask(); 0
483 Register Dst = MI.getOperand(0).getReg(); 0
484 int NumElts = MRI.getType(Dst).getNumElements(); 0
485 auto DstIsLeftAndDstLane = isINSMask(ShuffleMask, NumElts); 0
486 if (!DstIsLeftAndDstLane) 0
487 return false; 0
488 bool DstIsLeft; ----
489 int DstLane; ----
490 std::tie(DstIsLeft, DstLane) = *DstIsLeftAndDstLane; 0
491 Register Left = MI.getOperand(1).getReg(); 0
492 Register Right = MI.getOperand(2).getReg(); 0
493 Register DstVec = DstIsLeft ? Left : Right; 0
494 Register SrcVec = Left; 0
495 ----
496 int SrcLane = ShuffleMask[DstLane]; 0
497 if (SrcLane >= NumElts) { 0
498 SrcVec = Right; 0
499 SrcLane -= NumElts; 0
500 } ----
501 ----
502 MatchInfo = std::make_tuple(DstVec, DstLane, SrcVec, SrcLane); 0
503 return true; 0
504 } ----
505 ----
506 void applyINS(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
507 MachineIRBuilder &Builder, ----
508 std::tuple &MatchInfo) { ----
509 Builder.setInstrAndDebugLoc(MI); 0
510 Register Dst = MI.getOperand(0).getReg(); 0
511 auto ScalarTy = MRI.getType(Dst).getElementType(); 0
512 Register DstVec, SrcVec; 0
513 int DstLane, SrcLane; ----
514 std::tie(DstVec, DstLane, SrcVec, SrcLane) = MatchInfo; 0
515 auto SrcCst = Builder.buildConstant(LLT::scalar(64), SrcLane); 0
516 auto Extract = Builder.buildExtractVectorElement(ScalarTy, SrcVec, SrcCst); 0
517 auto DstCst = Builder.buildConstant(LLT::scalar(64), DstLane); 0
518 Builder.buildInsertVectorElement(Dst, DstVec, Extract, DstCst); 0
519 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
520 } 0

522 /// isVShiftRImm - Check if this is a valid vector for the immediate ----
523 /// operand of a vector shift right operation. The value must be in the range: ----
524 /// 1 <= Value <= ElementBits for a right shift. ----
525 bool isVShiftRImm(Register Reg, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, LLT Ty, 0
526 int64_t &Cnt) { ----
527 assert(Ty.isVector() && "vector shift count is not a vector type"); 0
528 MachineInstr *MI = MRI.getVRegDef(Reg); 0
529 auto Cst = getAArch64VectorSplatScalar(*MI, MRI); 0
530 if (!Cst) 0
531 return false; 0
532 Cnt = *Cst; 0
533 int64_t ElementBits = Ty.getScalarSizeInBits(); 0
534 return Cnt >= 1 && Cnt <= ElementBits; 0
535 } ----
536 ----
537 /// Match a vector G_ASHR or G_LSHR with a valid immediate shift. ----
538 bool matchVAshrLshrImm(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
539 int64_t &Imm) { ----
540 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_ASHR || 0
541 MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_LSHR); ----
542 LLT Ty = MRI.getType(MI.getOperand(1).getReg()); 0
543 if (!Ty.isVector()) 0
544 return false; 0
545 return isVShiftRImm(MI.getOperand(2).getReg(), MRI, Ty, Imm); 0
546 } ----
547 ----
548 void applyVAshrLshrImm(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
549 int64_t &Imm) { ----
550 unsigned Opc = MI.getOpcode(); 0
551 assert(Opc == TargetOpcode::G_ASHR || Opc == TargetOpcode::G_LSHR); 0
552 unsigned NewOpc = 0
553 Opc == TargetOpcode::G_ASHR ? AArch64::G_VASHR : AArch64::G_VLSHR; 0
554 MachineIRBuilder MIB(MI); 0
555 auto ImmDef = MIB.buildConstant(LLT::scalar(32), Imm); 0
556 MIB.buildInstr(NewOpc, {MI.getOperand(0)}, {MI.getOperand(1), ImmDef}); 0
557 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
558 } 0
559 ----
560 /// Determine if it is possible to modify the \p RHS and predicate \p P of a ----
561 /// G_ICMP instruction such that the right-hand side is an arithmetic immediate. ----
562 /// ----
563 /// \returns A pair containing the updated immediate and predicate which may ----
564 /// be used to optimize the instruction. ----
565 /// ----
566 /// \note This assumes that the comparison has been legalized. ----
567 std::optional> ----
568 tryAdjustICmpImmAndPred(Register RHS, CmpInst::Predicate P, 0
569 const MachineRegisterInfo &MRI) { ----
570 const auto &Ty = MRI.getType(RHS); 0
571 if (Ty.isVector()) 0
572 return std::nullopt; 0
573 unsigned Size = Ty.getSizeInBits(); 0
574 assert((Size == 32 || Size == 64) && "Expected 32 or 64 bit compare only?"); 0
575 ----
576 // If the RHS is not a constant, or the RHS is already a valid arithmetic ----
577 // immediate, then there is nothing to change. ----
578 auto ValAndVReg = getIConstantVRegValWithLookThrough(RHS, MRI); 0
579 if (!ValAndVReg) 0
580 return std::nullopt; 0
581 uint64_t C = ValAndVReg->Value.getZExtValue(); 0
582 if (isLegalArithImmed(C)) 0
583 return std::nullopt; 0
584 ----
585 // We have a non-arithmetic immediate. Check if adjusting the immediate and ----
586 // adjusting the predicate will result in a legal arithmetic immediate. ----
587 switch (P) { 0
588 default: 0
589 return std::nullopt; 0
590 case CmpInst::ICMP_SLT: 0
591 case CmpInst::ICMP_SGE: ----
592 // Check for ----
593 // ----
594 // x slt c => x sle c - 1 ----
595 // x sge c => x sgt c - 1 ----
596 // ----
597 // When c is not the smallest possible negative number. ----
598 if ((Size == 64 && static_cast(C) == INT64_MIN) || 0
599 (Size == 32 && static_cast(C) == INT32_MIN)) 0
600 return std::nullopt; 0
601 P = (P == CmpInst::ICMP_SLT) ? CmpInst::ICMP_SLE : CmpInst::ICMP_SGT; 0
602 C -= 1; 0
603 break; 0
604 case CmpInst::ICMP_ULT: 0
605 case CmpInst::ICMP_UGE: ----
606 // Check for ----
607 // ----
608 // x ult c => x ule c - 1 ----
609 // x uge c => x ugt c - 1 ----
610 // ----
611 // When c is not zero. ----
612 if (C == 0) 0
613 return std::nullopt; 0
614 P = (P == CmpInst::ICMP_ULT) ? CmpInst::ICMP_ULE : CmpInst::ICMP_UGT; 0
615 C -= 1; 0
616 break; 0
617 case CmpInst::ICMP_SLE: 0
618 case CmpInst::ICMP_SGT: ----
619 // Check for ----
620 // ----
621 // x sle c => x slt c + 1 ----
622 // x sgt c => s sge c + 1 ----
623 // ----
624 // When c is not the largest possible signed integer. ----
625 if ((Size == 32 && static_cast(C) == INT32_MAX) || 0
626 (Size == 64 && static_cast(C) == INT64_MAX)) 0
627 return std::nullopt; 0
628 P = (P == CmpInst::ICMP_SLE) ? CmpInst::ICMP_SLT : CmpInst::ICMP_SGE; 0
629 C += 1; 0
630 break; 0
631 case CmpInst::ICMP_ULE: 0
632 case CmpInst::ICMP_UGT: ----
633 // Check for ----
634 // ----
635 // x ule c => x ult c + 1 ----
636 // x ugt c => s uge c + 1 ----
637 // ----
638 // When c is not the largest possible unsigned integer. ----
639 if ((Size == 32 && static_cast(C) == UINT32_MAX) || 0
640 (Size == 64 && C == UINT64_MAX)) 0
641 return std::nullopt; 0
642 P = (P == CmpInst::ICMP_ULE) ? CmpInst::ICMP_ULT : CmpInst::ICMP_UGE; 0
643 C += 1; 0
644 break; 0
645 } ----
646 ----
647 // Check if the new constant is valid, and return the updated constant and ----
648 // predicate if it is. ----
649 if (Size == 32) 0
650 C = static_cast(C); 0
651 if (!isLegalArithImmed(C)) 0
652 return std::nullopt; 0
653 return {{C, P}}; 0
654 } 0
655 ----
656 /// Determine whether or not it is possible to update the RHS and predicate of ----
657 /// a G_ICMP instruction such that the RHS will be selected as an arithmetic ----
658 /// immediate. ----
659 /// ----
660 /// \p MI - The G_ICMP instruction ----
661 /// \p MatchInfo - The new RHS immediate and predicate on success ----
662 /// ----
663 /// See tryAdjustICmpImmAndPred for valid transformations. ----
664 bool matchAdjustICmpImmAndPred( 0
665 MachineInstr &MI, const MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, ----
666 std::pair &MatchInfo) { ----
667 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_ICMP); 0
668 Register RHS = MI.getOperand(3).getReg(); 0
669 auto Pred = static_cast(MI.getOperand(1).getPredicate()); 0
670 if (auto MaybeNewImmAndPred = tryAdjustICmpImmAndPred(RHS, Pred, MRI)) { 0
671 MatchInfo = *MaybeNewImmAndPred; 0
672 return true; 0
673 } ----
674 return false; 0
675 } ----
676 ----
677 void applyAdjustICmpImmAndPred( 0
678 MachineInstr &MI, std::pair &MatchInfo, ----
679 MachineIRBuilder &MIB, GISelChangeObserver &Observer) { ----
680 MIB.setInstrAndDebugLoc(MI); 0
681 MachineOperand &RHS = MI.getOperand(3); 0
682 MachineRegisterInfo &MRI = *MIB.getMRI(); 0
683 auto Cst = MIB.buildConstant(MRI.cloneVirtualRegister(RHS.getReg()), 0
684 MatchInfo.first); 0
685 Observer.changingInstr(MI); 0
686 RHS.setReg(Cst->getOperand(0).getReg()); 0
687 MI.getOperand(1).setPredicate(MatchInfo.second); 0
688 Observer.changedInstr(MI); 0
689 } 0
690 ----
691 bool matchDupLane(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
692 std::pair &MatchInfo) { ----
693 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR); 0
694 Register Src1Reg = MI.getOperand(1).getReg(); 0
695 const LLT SrcTy = MRI.getType(Src1Reg); 0
696 const LLT DstTy = MRI.getType(MI.getOperand(0).getReg()); 0
697 ----
698 auto LaneIdx = getSplatIndex(MI); 0
699 if (!LaneIdx) 0
700 return false; 0
701 ----
702 // The lane idx should be within the first source vector. ----
703 if (*LaneIdx >= SrcTy.getNumElements()) 0
704 return false; 0
705 ----
706 if (DstTy != SrcTy) 0
707 return false; 0
708 ----
709 LLT ScalarTy = SrcTy.getElementType(); 0
710 unsigned ScalarSize = ScalarTy.getSizeInBits(); 0
711 ----
712 unsigned Opc = 0; 0
713 switch (SrcTy.getNumElements()) { 0
714 case 2: 0
715 if (ScalarSize == 64) 0
716 Opc = AArch64::G_DUPLANE64; 0
717 else if (ScalarSize == 32) 0
718 Opc = AArch64::G_DUPLANE32; 0
719 break; 0
720 case 4: 0
721 if (ScalarSize == 32) 0
722 Opc = AArch64::G_DUPLANE32; 0
723 break; 0
724 case 8: 0
725 if (ScalarSize == 16) 0
726 Opc = AArch64::G_DUPLANE16; 0
727 break; 0
728 case 16: 0
729 if (ScalarSize == 8) 0
730 Opc = AArch64::G_DUPLANE8; 0
731 break; 0
732 default: 0
733 break; 0
734 } ----
735 if (!Opc) 0
736 return false; 0
737 ----
738 MatchInfo.first = Opc; 0
739 MatchInfo.second = *LaneIdx; 0
740 return true; 0
741 } ----
742 ----
743 void applyDupLane(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
744 MachineIRBuilder &B, std::pair &MatchInfo) { ----
745 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SHUFFLE_VECTOR); 0
746 Register Src1Reg = MI.getOperand(1).getReg(); 0
747 const LLT SrcTy = MRI.getType(Src1Reg); 0
748 ----
749 B.setInstrAndDebugLoc(MI); 0
750 auto Lane = B.buildConstant(LLT::scalar(64), MatchInfo.second); 0
751 ----
752 Register DupSrc = MI.getOperand(1).getReg(); 0
753 // For types like <2 x s32>, we can use G_DUPLANE32, with a <4 x s32> source. ----
754 // To do this, we can use a G_CONCAT_VECTORS to do the widening. ----
755 if (SrcTy == LLT::fixed_vector(2, LLT::scalar(32))) { 0
756 assert(MRI.getType(MI.getOperand(0).getReg()).getNumElements() == 2 && 0
757 "Unexpected dest elements"); ----
758 auto Undef = B.buildUndef(SrcTy); 0
759 DupSrc = B.buildConcatVectors( 0
760 SrcTy.changeElementCount(ElementCount::getFixed(4)), ----
761 {Src1Reg, Undef.getReg(0)}) 0
762 .getReg(0); 0
763 } ----
764 B.buildInstr(MatchInfo.first, {MI.getOperand(0).getReg()}, {DupSrc, Lane}); 0
765 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
766 } 0
767 ----
768 bool matchBuildVectorToDup(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI) { 0
769 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_BUILD_VECTOR); 0
770 auto Splat = getAArch64VectorSplat(MI, MRI); 0
771 if (!Splat) 0
772 return false; 0
773 if (Splat->isReg()) 0
774 return true; 0
775 // Later, during selection, we'll try to match imported patterns using ----
776 // immAllOnesV and immAllZerosV. These require G_BUILD_VECTOR. Don't lower ----
777 // G_BUILD_VECTORs which could match those patterns. ----
778 int64_t Cst = Splat->getCst(); 0
779 return (Cst != 0 && Cst != -1); 0
780 } ----
781 ----
782 void applyBuildVectorToDup(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
783 MachineIRBuilder &B) { ----
784 B.setInstrAndDebugLoc(MI); 0
785 B.buildInstr(AArch64::G_DUP, {MI.getOperand(0).getReg()}, 0
786 {MI.getOperand(1).getReg()}); 0
787 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
788 } 0
789 ----
790 /// \returns how many instructions would be saved by folding a G_ICMP's shift ----
791 /// and/or extension operations. ----
792 unsigned getCmpOperandFoldingProfit(Register CmpOp, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI) { 0
793 // No instructions to save if there's more than one use or no uses. ----
794 if (!MRI.hasOneNonDBGUse(CmpOp)) 0
795 return 0; 0
796 ----
797 // FIXME: This is duplicated with the selector. (See: selectShiftedRegister) ----
798 auto IsSupportedExtend = [&](const MachineInstr &MI) { 0
799 if (MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SEXT_INREG) 0
800 return true; 0
801 if (MI.getOpcode() != TargetOpcode::G_AND) 0
802 return false; 0
803 auto ValAndVReg = ----
804 getIConstantVRegValWithLookThrough(MI.getOperand(2).getReg(), MRI); 0
805 if (!ValAndVReg) 0
806 return false; 0
807 uint64_t Mask = ValAndVReg->Value.getZExtValue(); 0
808 return (Mask == 0xFF || Mask == 0xFFFF || Mask == 0xFFFFFFFF); 0
809 }; 0
810 ----
811 MachineInstr *Def = getDefIgnoringCopies(CmpOp, MRI); 0
812 if (IsSupportedExtend(*Def)) 0
813 return 1; 0
814 ----
815 unsigned Opc = Def->getOpcode(); 0
816 if (Opc != TargetOpcode::G_SHL && Opc != TargetOpcode::G_ASHR && 0
817 Opc != TargetOpcode::G_LSHR) ----
818 return 0; 0
819 ----
820 auto MaybeShiftAmt = ----
821 getIConstantVRegValWithLookThrough(Def->getOperand(2).getReg(), MRI); 0
822 if (!MaybeShiftAmt) 0
823 return 0; 0
824 uint64_t ShiftAmt = MaybeShiftAmt->Value.getZExtValue(); 0
825 MachineInstr *ShiftLHS = ----
826 getDefIgnoringCopies(Def->getOperand(1).getReg(), MRI); 0
827 ----
828 // Check if we can fold an extend and a shift. ----
829 // FIXME: This is duplicated with the selector. (See: ----
830 // selectArithExtendedRegister) ----
831 if (IsSupportedExtend(*ShiftLHS)) 0
832 return (ShiftAmt <= 4) ? 2 : 1; 0
833 ----
834 LLT Ty = MRI.getType(Def->getOperand(0).getReg()); 0
835 if (Ty.isVector()) 0
836 return 0; 0
837 unsigned ShiftSize = Ty.getSizeInBits(); 0
838 if ((ShiftSize == 32 && ShiftAmt <= 31) || 0
839 (ShiftSize == 64 && ShiftAmt <= 63)) 0
840 return 1; 0
841 return 0; 0
842 } 0
843 ----
844 /// \returns true if it would be profitable to swap the LHS and RHS of a G_ICMP ----
845 /// instruction \p MI. ----
846 bool trySwapICmpOperands(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI) { 0
847 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_ICMP); 0
848 // Swap the operands if it would introduce a profitable folding opportunity. ----
849 // (e.g. a shift + extend). ----
850 // ----
851 // For example: ----
852 // lsl w13, w11, #1 ----
853 // cmp w13, w12 ----
854 // can be turned into: ----
855 // cmp w12, w11, lsl #1 ----
856 ----
857 // Don't swap if there's a constant on the RHS, because we know we can fold ----
858 // that. ----
859 Register RHS = MI.getOperand(3).getReg(); 0
860 auto RHSCst = getIConstantVRegValWithLookThrough(RHS, MRI); 0
861 if (RHSCst && isLegalArithImmed(RHSCst->Value.getSExtValue())) 0
862 return false; 0
863 ----
864 Register LHS = MI.getOperand(2).getReg(); 0
865 auto Pred = static_cast(MI.getOperand(1).getPredicate()); 0
866 auto GetRegForProfit = [&](Register Reg) { 0
867 MachineInstr *Def = getDefIgnoringCopies(Reg, MRI); 0
868 return isCMN(Def, Pred, MRI) ? Def->getOperand(2).getReg() : Reg; 0
869 }; 0
870 ----
871 // Don't have a constant on the RHS. If we swap the LHS and RHS of the ----
872 // compare, would we be able to fold more instructions? ----
873 Register TheLHS = GetRegForProfit(LHS); 0
874 Register TheRHS = GetRegForProfit(RHS); 0
875 ----
876 // If the LHS is more likely to give us a folding opportunity, then swap the ----
877 // LHS and RHS. ----
878 return (getCmpOperandFoldingProfit(TheLHS, MRI) > 0
879 getCmpOperandFoldingProfit(TheRHS, MRI)); 0
880 } 0
881 ----
882 void applySwapICmpOperands(MachineInstr &MI, GISelChangeObserver &Observer) { 0
883 auto Pred = static_cast(MI.getOperand(1).getPredicate()); 0
884 Register LHS = MI.getOperand(2).getReg(); 0
885 Register RHS = MI.getOperand(3).getReg(); 0
886 Observer.changedInstr(MI); 0
887 MI.getOperand(1).setPredicate(CmpInst::getSwappedPredicate(Pred)); 0
888 MI.getOperand(2).setReg(RHS); 0
889 MI.getOperand(3).setReg(LHS); 0
890 Observer.changedInstr(MI); 0
891 } 0
892 ----
893 /// \returns a function which builds a vector floating point compare instruction ----
894 /// for a condition code \p CC. ----
895 /// \param [in] IsZero - True if the comparison is against 0. ----
896 /// \param [in] NoNans - True if the target has NoNansFPMath. ----
897 std::function ----
898 getVectorFCMP(AArch64CC::CondCode CC, Register LHS, Register RHS, bool IsZero, 0
899 bool NoNans, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI) { ----
900 LLT DstTy = MRI.getType(LHS); 0
901 assert(DstTy.isVector() && "Expected vector types only?"); 0
902 assert(DstTy == MRI.getType(RHS) && "Src and Dst types must match!"); 0
903 switch (CC) { 0
904 default: 0
905 llvm_unreachable("Unexpected condition code!"); 0
906 case AArch64CC::NE: 0
907 return [LHS, RHS, IsZero, DstTy](MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { 0
908 auto FCmp = IsZero ----
909 ? MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMEQZ, {DstTy}, {LHS}) 0
910 : MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMEQ, {DstTy}, {LHS, RHS}); 0
911 return MIB.buildNot(DstTy, FCmp).getReg(0); 0
912 }; 0
913 case AArch64CC::EQ: 0
914 return [LHS, RHS, IsZero, DstTy](MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { 0
915 return IsZero ----
916 ? MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMEQZ, {DstTy}, {LHS}).getReg(0) 0
917 : MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMEQ, {DstTy}, {LHS, RHS}) 0
918 .getReg(0); 0
919 }; 0
920 case AArch64CC::GE: 0
921 return [LHS, RHS, IsZero, DstTy](MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { 0
922 return IsZero ----
923 ? MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMGEZ, {DstTy}, {LHS}).getReg(0) 0
924 : MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMGE, {DstTy}, {LHS, RHS}) 0
925 .getReg(0); 0
926 }; 0
927 case AArch64CC::GT: 0
928 return [LHS, RHS, IsZero, DstTy](MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { 0
929 return IsZero ----
930 ? MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMGTZ, {DstTy}, {LHS}).getReg(0) 0
931 : MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMGT, {DstTy}, {LHS, RHS}) 0
932 .getReg(0); 0
933 }; 0
934 case AArch64CC::LS: 0
935 return [LHS, RHS, IsZero, DstTy](MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { 0
936 return IsZero ----
937 ? MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMLEZ, {DstTy}, {LHS}).getReg(0) 0
938 : MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMGE, {DstTy}, {RHS, LHS}) 0
939 .getReg(0); 0
940 }; 0
941 case AArch64CC::MI: 0
942 return [LHS, RHS, IsZero, DstTy](MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { 0
943 return IsZero ----
944 ? MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMLTZ, {DstTy}, {LHS}).getReg(0) 0
945 : MIB.buildInstr(AArch64::G_FCMGT, {DstTy}, {RHS, LHS}) 0
946 .getReg(0); 0
947 }; 0
948 } ----
949 } ----
950 ----
951 /// Try to lower a vector G_FCMP \p MI into an AArch64-specific pseudo. ----
952 bool matchLowerVectorFCMP(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
953 MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { ----
954 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_FCMP); 0
955 const auto &ST = MI.getMF()->getSubtarget(); 0
956 ----
957 Register Dst = MI.getOperand(0).getReg(); 0
958 LLT DstTy = MRI.getType(Dst); 0
959 if (!DstTy.isVector() || !ST.hasNEON()) 0
960 return false; 0
961 Register LHS = MI.getOperand(2).getReg(); 0
962 unsigned EltSize = MRI.getType(LHS).getScalarSizeInBits(); 0
963 if (EltSize == 16 && !ST.hasFullFP16()) 0
964 return false; 0
965 if (EltSize != 16 && EltSize != 32 && EltSize != 64) 0
966 return false; 0
967 ----
968 return true; 0
969 } ----
970 ----
971 /// Try to lower a vector G_FCMP \p MI into an AArch64-specific pseudo. ----
972 void applyLowerVectorFCMP(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
973 MachineIRBuilder &MIB) { ----
974 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_FCMP); 0
975 const auto &ST = MI.getMF()->getSubtarget(); 0
976 ----
977 const auto &CmpMI = cast(MI); 0
978 ----
979 Register Dst = CmpMI.getReg(0); 0
980 CmpInst::Predicate Pred = CmpMI.getCond(); 0
981 Register LHS = CmpMI.getLHSReg(); 0
982 Register RHS = CmpMI.getRHSReg(); 0
983 ----
984 LLT DstTy = MRI.getType(Dst); 0
985 ----
986 auto Splat = getAArch64VectorSplat(*MRI.getVRegDef(RHS), MRI); 0
987 ----
988 // Compares against 0 have special target-specific pseudos. ----
989 bool IsZero = Splat && Splat->isCst() && Splat->getCst() == 0; 0
990 ----
991 bool Invert = false; 0
992 AArch64CC::CondCode CC, CC2 = AArch64CC::AL; 0
993 if (Pred == CmpInst::Predicate::FCMP_ORD && IsZero) { 0
994 // The special case "fcmp ord %a, 0" is the canonical check that LHS isn't ----
995 // NaN, so equivalent to a == a and doesn't need the two comparisons an ----
996 // "ord" normally would. ----
997 RHS = LHS; 0
998 IsZero = false; 0
999 CC = AArch64CC::EQ; 0
1000 } else ----
1001 changeVectorFCMPPredToAArch64CC(Pred, CC, CC2, Invert); 0
1002 ----
1003 // Instead of having an apply function, just build here to simplify things. ----
1004 MIB.setInstrAndDebugLoc(MI); 0
1005 ----
1006 const bool NoNans = ----
1007 ST.getTargetLowering()->getTargetMachine().Options.NoNaNsFPMath; 0
1008 ----
1009 auto Cmp = getVectorFCMP(CC, LHS, RHS, IsZero, NoNans, MRI); 0
1010 Register CmpRes; 0
1011 if (CC2 == AArch64CC::AL) 0
1012 CmpRes = Cmp(MIB); 0
1013 else { ----
1014 auto Cmp2 = getVectorFCMP(CC2, LHS, RHS, IsZero, NoNans, MRI); 0
1015 auto Cmp2Dst = Cmp2(MIB); 0
1016 auto Cmp1Dst = Cmp(MIB); 0
1017 CmpRes = MIB.buildOr(DstTy, Cmp1Dst, Cmp2Dst).getReg(0); 0
1018 } 0
1019 if (Invert) 0
1020 CmpRes = MIB.buildNot(DstTy, CmpRes).getReg(0); 0
1021 MRI.replaceRegWith(Dst, CmpRes); 0
1022 MI.eraseFromParent(); 0
1023 } 0
1024 ----
1025 bool matchFormTruncstore(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
1026 Register &SrcReg) { ----
1027 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_STORE); 0
1028 Register DstReg = MI.getOperand(0).getReg(); 0
1029 if (MRI.getType(DstReg).isVector()) 0
1030 return false; 0
1031 // Match a store of a truncate. ----
1032 if (!mi_match(DstReg, MRI, m_GTrunc(m_Reg(SrcReg)))) 0
1033 return false; 0
1034 // Only form truncstores for value types of max 64b. ----
1035 return MRI.getType(SrcReg).getSizeInBits() <= 64; 0
1036 } ----
1037 ----
1038 void applyFormTruncstore(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
1039 MachineIRBuilder &B, GISelChangeObserver &Observer, ----
1040 Register &SrcReg) { ----
1041 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_STORE); 0
1042 Observer.changingInstr(MI); 0
1043 MI.getOperand(0).setReg(SrcReg); 0
1044 Observer.changedInstr(MI); 0
1045 } 0

1047 // Lower vector G_SEXT_INREG back to shifts for selection. We allowed them to ----
1048 // form in the first place for combine opportunities, so any remaining ones ----
1049 // at this stage need be lowered back. ----
1050 bool matchVectorSextInReg(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI) { 0
1051 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SEXT_INREG); 0
1052 Register DstReg = MI.getOperand(0).getReg(); 0
1053 LLT DstTy = MRI.getType(DstReg); 0
1054 return DstTy.isVector(); 0
1055 } ----
1056 ----
1057 void applyVectorSextInReg(MachineInstr &MI, MachineRegisterInfo &MRI, 0
1058 MachineIRBuilder &B, GISelChangeObserver &Observer) { ----
1059 assert(MI.getOpcode() == TargetOpcode::G_SEXT_INREG); 0
1060 B.setInstrAndDebugLoc(MI); 0
1061 LegalizerHelper Helper(*MI.getMF(), Observer, B); 0
1062 Helper.lower(MI, 0, /* Unused hint type */ LLT()); 0
1063 } 0
1064 ----
1065 class AArch64PostLegalizerLoweringImpl : public GIMatchTableExecutor { ----
1066 protected: ----
1067 CombinerHelper &Helper; ----
1068 const AArch64PostLegalizerLoweringImplRuleConfig &RuleConfig; ----
1069 ----
1070 const AArch64Subtarget &STI; ----
1071 GISelChangeObserver &Observer; ----
1072 MachineIRBuilder &B; ----
1073 MachineFunction &MF; ----
